  <section class="artdeco-card p4 mb3">
    <h4 class="t-20 t-black t-bold mb2">
      Overview
    </h4>

      <p class="break-words white-space-pre-wrap mb5 t-14 t-black--light t-normal">ON Animation Studios is a winning feature animation studio with a mission to continue to create compelling, heartwarming stories through innovation, technology, and international talent. 

Based in Montreal since 2012, ON Animation Studios became the home of the technical and artistic team that developed and produced the Cesar Award-winning film The Little Prince, Mune: Guardian of the Moon and Playmobil the Movie.

ON Animation Studios is currently working on its next adventure on the much anticipated: Ladybug &amp; Cat Noir Awakening (based on the international series sensation Miraculous Ladybug).

Follow this profile to keep up to date with ON Animation Studio!

-

ON Animation Studios est un studio d'animation de long mtrage qui a pour mission de combiner innovation, technologie et talents internationaux au service dunivers feriques et merveilleux pour les enfants et la famille.

Bas  Montral depuis 2012, ON Animation Studios est devenu le foyer de l'quipe technique et artistique qui a dvelopp et produit les films Le Petit Prince (Csar du meilleur film danimation), Mune le gardien de la lune et Playmobil le film.

ON Animation Studios travaille actuellement sur sa prochaine aventure sur le trs attendu film Ladybug &amp; Cat Noir Awakening (bas sur le succs international Miraculous Ladybug).

Suivez ce profil pour rester  jour avec ON Animation Studio!</p>
